# üé¨ Screen Tests

**Film Studio**
Est. 2025 ¬∑ Every 15 Minutes

---

## üéûÔ∏è The Archive

Warhol filmed people. We film code.

Each repository is a subject. Silent. Still. Frozen in time.

Camera #0 never stops. Every 15 minutes. New film. New reel.

---

## üé• Now Showing

| Reel | Subject | Genre | Recorded |
|------|---------|-------|----------|
| #2114 | [RapidAI/RapidOCR](https://github.com/RapidAI/RapidOCR) | Python ¬∑ ‚≠ê 5k | 2025-12-09 |
---

## üé≠ Selection Process

```
40% Trending
30% Classics
20% Indies
10% Experimental
```

Random. Automatic. Continuous.

---

## üì¶ Requests

Want your repo recorded?

üìß **hi@sdpkjc.com**

---

## üîß Run Your Own

```bash
pip install -r requirements.txt
export GITHUB_TOKEN="your-token"
python camera0.py  # Start Camera #0
```

Or let GitHub Action run it automatically.
